Criterion Api:- 
 SRO hibernate persistence methods 
 bulkoperations - we use HQL(query written using classname and properties) to write queries. 
 In case of Criterion api, we can perform both singlerow and bulkoperations without using any queries just 
like java statements. 
 Criterion api will generate SQL queries based on the given entity classnames and properties name. 
 It doesnot support non-select operation,it supports only select operation. 
 Using Criteria object we can add 3 object 
 
a. Criterion objects(for where clause condition) 
b. Project objects(for scalar select operation) 
c. Order object( for orderBy operations) 
 
There are 2 modes of writing Criterion api 
a. HB QBC(Query by Criteria)====> specific to hibernate only 
b. JPA QBC ===> common to all ORM framework 
refer: HBQBCApi 
 
What is CriteriaBuilder? 
CriteriaBuilder is a factory for building different parts of a Criteria API query in Java. 
Think of it like a toolbox that gives you tools (methods) to create: 
SELECT queries 
UPDATE queries 
DELETE queries 
Expressions (e.g., conditions, comparisons, arithmetic, etc.) 
It’s part of JPA (Java Persistence API), and it's usually obtained from the EntityManager or Session object in Hibernate. 
 
package com.CriteriaApi; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.query.Query; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaBuilder; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaQuery; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Root; 
public class CriterianGetMobiles { 
    public static void main(String[] args) { 
        Session session = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
        try { 
            //Step 1 : Get CriteriaBuilder.... 
         CriteriaBuilder criteriaBuilder = session.getCriteriaBuilder(); 
         //Step2 : Create Criteria Query.... 
         CriteriaQuery<MobilesProductsEntity> cq = 
criteriaBuilder.createQuery(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
         //Step3 : Define from Class root... 
         Root<MobilesProductsEntity> root = cq.from(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
         // Step 4: Set SELECT (optional, selects whole entity here) 
         cq.select(root); 
          
           //Step 5 : create Query need to execute.... 
         Query<MobilesProductsEntity> query = session.createQuery(cq); 
         List<MobilesProductsEntity> list = query.getResultList(); 
         // Step 6: Print results 
         list.forEach(System.out::println); 
        } catch (Exception e) { 
            e.printStackTrace(); 
        } finally { 
            session.close(); 
        } 
    } 
}

✅ When to Use Criteria API? 
 When you need dynamic query 
construction at runtime. 
 When you want type safety 
(checked at compile time). 
 When building complex queries 
programmatically. 
 
   
  
 
Select Query Code With Filter Condiation: 
package com.CriteriaApi; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.query.Query; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaBuilder; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaQuery; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Root; 
public class CriterianSelectConditation { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  Session session = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
  try { 
   //Step 1: Creating Criterian Builder and Criterian Query... 
   CriteriaBuilder cb  = session.getCriteriaBuilder(); 
   CriteriaQuery<MobilesProductsEntity> cq =  
cb.createQuery(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
    
   // Step 2: Defines from clause and applying the were conditation.. 
   Root<MobilesProductsEntity> root = cq.from(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
    
   cq.select(root).where( 
     cb.and( 
       cb.greaterThan(root.get("offerPrice"), 10000), 
       cb.lessThan(root.get("offerPrice"), 12000) 
        ) 
   ).orderBy(cb.asc(root.get("offerPrice"))); 
    
   //Step 3 : Executing the Query... 
   Query<MobilesProductsEntity> query = session.createQuery(cq); 
   List<MobilesProductsEntity>  list = query.getResultList(); 
   list.forEach(System.out::println); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
 } 
}

Criteria API, Tuple is a special type that represents a row of selected column 
values when you're not selecting the full entity, but only specific fields 
(projections). 
 
�
� What is Tuple? 
 Tuple is an interface in jakarta.persistence. 
 It is used when you want to fetch multiple columns, but not an entire 
entity object. 
 Each row is represented as a Tuple object. 
 Each column (field) inside a row can be accessed using: 
 tuple.get(int index) → by position 
 tuple.get(String alias) → by alias name 
 
  
 
package com.CriteriaApi; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.query.Query; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
import jakarta.persistence.Tuple; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaBuilder; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaQuery; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Root; 
public class CriterianMultySelectColumn { 
  public static void main(String[] args) { 
 Session session = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
 try { 
  // Step 1: Get CriteriaBuilder 
  CriteriaBuilder cb  = session.getCriteriaBuilder(); 
   // Step 2: Create CriteriaQuery for Tuple (for partial selection) 
  CriteriaQuery<Tuple> cq =  cb.createTupleQuery(); 
   // Step 3: Define FROM clause 
  Root<MobilesProductsEntity> root =  cq.from(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
   // Step 4: Select only required fields with alias 
  cq.multiselect( 
    root.get("productTitle").alias("Title"), 
    root.get("brand").alias("Brand"), 
    root.get("offerPrice").alias("OfferPrice"), 
    root.get("originalPrice").alias("OriginalPrice") 
   ).where( 
     cb.and( 
     cb.greaterThan(root.get("offerPrice"), 15000), 
     cb.lessThan(root.get("offerPrice"), 20000) 
     ) 
   ).orderBy(cb.asc(root.get("offerPrice"))); 
  // Step 5: Execute query 
  Query<Tuple> query = session.createQuery(cq); 
  List<Tuple> list = query.getResultList(); 
  for(Tuple tuple : list) 
  { 
   System.out.println( 
   "Title: \t"+ tuple.get("Title")+"\t|\t"+ 
   "Brand: \t"+tuple.get("Brand")+"\t|\t"+ 
   "OfferPrice: \t"+tuple.get("OfferPrice")+"\t|\t"+ 
   "OriginalPrice: \t"+tuple.get("OriginalPrice")); 
  } 
 } catch (Exception e) { 
  e.printStackTrace(); 
 } 
  
}

By Using Creatrin Api Updateing the Record from the Table : 
package com.CriteriaApi; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.Transaction; 
import org.hibernate.query.Query; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.PremiumMobilesProductEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaBuilder; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaUpdate; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Root; 
public class CriterianUpdateCode { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  Session session  = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
  Transaction transection = null; 
  int count = 0; 
  boolean flag = false; 
  try { 
   transection = session.beginTransaction(); 
   CriteriaBuilder cb  = session.getCriteriaBuilder(); 
   CriteriaUpdate<PremiumMobilesProductEntity> cu = 
cb.createCriteriaUpdate(PremiumMobilesProductEntity.class); 
   Root<PremiumMobilesProductEntity> root =  
cu.from(PremiumMobilesProductEntity.class); 
    
   cu.set(root.get("stockAvailability"), "No"); 
   cu.where( 
     cb.and( 
       cb.equal(root.get("sid"), 58) 
        ) 
     ); 
   Query<?> query = session.createQuery(cu); 
   count = query.executeUpdate(); 
   flag = true; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  finally { 
   if(flag) 
   { 
    transection.commit(); 
    System.out.println("No of rows effected :: "+count); 
   }else 
   { 
    transection.rollback(); 
    System.out.println("record doesnt exits or data not avalible...!"); 
   } 
  } 
 } 
}

Pagination:- 
Displaying large volume of records into muliptle pages is called as "pagination". 
Hibernate supports pagination through QBC 
1. setFirstResult(int pageNo) 
2. setMaxResult(int maxNo)  
 
package com.CriteriaApi; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.query.Query; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaBuilder; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.CriteriaQuery; 
import jakarta.persistence.criteria.Root; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
import java.util.List; 
public class PaginatedProducts { 
    public static void main(String[] args) { 
        int pageNumber = 1;     // page index (0-based) 
        int pageSize = 5;       // records per page 
 
        Session session = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
        try { 
            CriteriaBuilder cb = session.getCriteriaBuilder(); 
            CriteriaQuery<MobilesProductsEntity> cq = cb.createQuery(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
            Root<MobilesProductsEntity> root = cq.from(MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
 
            cq.select(root).orderBy(cb.asc(root.get("offerPrice"))); // optional sorting 
 
            Query<MobilesProductsEntity> query = session.createQuery(cq); 
            query.setFirstResult(pageNumber * pageSize); // e.g., 0, 5, 10... 
            query.setMaxResults(pageSize); 
 
            List<MobilesProductsEntity> result = query.getResultList(); 
            result.forEach(System.out::println); 
 
        } catch (Exception e) { 
            e.printStackTrace(); 
        } finally { 
            session.close(); 
        } 
    } 
}

StoredProcedure calls in hibernate:- 
1. we use ProcedureCall(I) to make a call to storedprocedure 
2. we use ParameterMode(Enum) to specify the IN,OUT,INOUT Param 
  
To get all the columns value data in the form of ResultSet:- 
 ProcedureCall procedureCall = 
 session.createStoredProcedureCall("GET_POLICIES_BY_TENURE",InsurancePolicy.clas
s); 
 procedureCall.registerParameter(1, Integer.class, 
 ParameterMode.IN).bindValue(start); 
 procedureCall.registerParameter(2, Integer.class, ParameterMode.IN).bindValue(end); 
 List<InsurancePolicy> list = procedureCall.getResultList(); 
 To get specific columns based on the input type 
 
  
 
  
 
2. Hibernate Supports Stored Procedures via: 
StoredProcedureQuery (JPA standard – recommended) 
 
ProcedureCall (Hibernate-specific – avoid unless needed) 
 
Dao Interface:- 
package com.StoreProceduresHandeling; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
public interface MobileProductDataIDao { 
 List<MobilesProductsEntity> getAllProductDetailsInfo(String brand); 
 List<Object[]> getProductDetailsInfo(String brand); 
} 
 
package com.StoreProceduresHandeling; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
import jakarta.persistence.ParameterMode; 
import jakarta.persistence.StoredProcedureQuery; 
 /*DELIMITER // 
 CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `GetAllProductInfo`( 
     IN brand_name VARCHAR(150) 
 ) 
 BEGIN 
     SELECT *   FROM flipkart_mobile_data  WHERE brand = brand_name; 
 END // 
 DELIMITER ;*/ 
public class MobileProductImpl implements MobileProductDataIDao { 
 
 @Override 
 public List<MobilesProductsEntity> getAllProductDetailsInfo(String brand) { 
   Session session = null; 
   List<MobilesProductsEntity> list = new ArrayList<MobilesProductsEntity>(); 
         try { 
             session = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
             
             if (session != null) { 
                 // Creating StoredProcedureQuery instead of ProcedureCall 
                 StoredProcedureQuery procedureQuery = session 
                     .createStoredProcedureQuery("GetAllProductInfo", 
MobilesProductsEntity.class); 
 
                 // Register input parameter with mode 
                 procedureQuery.registerStoredProcedureParameter(1, String.class, 
ParameterMode.IN); 
                 procedureQuery.setParameter(1, brand); 
 
                 // Get result list 
                 list = procedureQuery.getResultList(); 
                 list.forEach(System.out::println); 
             } 
         } catch (Exception e) { 
             e.printStackTrace(); 
         } finally { 
             HibernateUtil.CloseSession(session); 
         } 
   return list; 
 } 
 
Dao Implementation 
 
  
 
/*CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `GetBasicProductInfo`( 
    IN brand_name VARCHAR(150) 
) 
BEGIN 
    SELECT  
        sid, 
        product_title, 
        brand, 
        offer_price, 
        original_price, 
        product_rating AS rating, 
         CASE 
            WHEN offer_price = 0 THEN 0 
        ELSE ROUND(((original_price - offer_price) / original_price) * 100, 2) END AS 
discount 
    FROM 
        flipkart_mobile_data 
    WHERE 
        brand = brand_name; 
END*/ 
 @Override 
 public List<Object[]> getProductDetailsInfo(String brand) { 
  Session session = null; 
   List<Object[]> list = new ArrayList<Object[]>(); 
         try { 
             session = HibernateUtil.getSession(); 
             
             if (session != null) { 
                 // Creating StoredProcedureQuery instead of ProcedureCall 
                 StoredProcedureQuery procedureQuery = session 
                     .createStoredProcedureQuery("GetBasicProductInfo"); 
 
                 // Register input parameter with mode 
                 procedureQuery.registerStoredProcedureParameter(1, String.class, 
ParameterMode.IN); 
                 procedureQuery.setParameter(1, brand); 
 
                 // Get result list 
                 list = procedureQuery.getResultList(); 
                 list.forEach(row-> 
                 { 
                  StringBuffer bf= new StringBuffer(); 
                  for(Object obj : row) 
                  { 
                   if(bf.length()>0) 
                   { 
                    bf.append(" <----> "); 
                   } 
                   bf.append(obj); 
                  } 
                   System.out.println("Out Put : "+ bf.toString()); 
                 });         
             } 
         } catch (Exception e) { 
             e.printStackTrace(); 
         } finally { 
             HibernateUtil.CloseSession(session); 
         } 
   return list; 
 } 
  
} 
 
package com.StoreProceduresHandeling;

import com.FirstHibernateProject.MobilesProductsEntity; 
import com.HibernateUtils.HibernateUtil; 
 
public class Mobilecontroller { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  MobileProductDataIDao mobdao = new MobileProductImpl(); 
  List<MobilesProductsEntity> listmob = mobdao.getAllProductDetailsInfo("POCO"); 
  HibernateUtil.closeSessionFactory();  
 } 
}
